{"type":"assistant","message":{"model":"claude-haiku-4-5-20251001","id":"msg_01XVy3ttGCnnfXaRkXyYzcTP","type":"message","role":"assistant","content":[{"type":"tool_use","id":"toolu_01LayKcjT6qfScakvhQe6WYz","name":"Write","input":{"file_path":"/workspace/regression_test.py","content":"\"\"\"Regression test for HSV color percentage parsing bug.\n\nThis test verifies that HSV and HSVA colors with percentage values\nare parsed correctly, with hue scaled to 0-359 degrees instead of 0-255.\n\nBug: When users specify colors using HSV notation with percentage values,\nthe hue component is incorrectly scaled using a maximum of 255 instead of 359.\n- hsv(100%, 100%, 100%) should parse to hue=359, not hue=255\n- hsv(50%, 50%, 50%) should parse to hue=179-180, not hue=127\n\"\"\"\n\nimport pytest\nfrom PyQt5.QtGui import QColor\nfrom qutebrowser.config import configtypes\n\n\nclass TestHSVPercentageBug:\n    \"\"\"Test for HSV percentage parsing regression.\"\"\"\n\n    def test_hsv_100_percent_hue(self):\n        \"\"\"Test that 100% hue is scaled to 359, not 255.\"\"\"\n        color_parser = configtypes.QtColor()\n        parsed_color = color_parser.to_py('hsv(100%, 100%, 100%)')\n\n        # Extract the hue value from the QColor object\n        hue = parsed_color.hue()\n        saturation = parsed_color.saturation()\n        value = parsed_color.value()\n\n        # Hue should be 359 (100% of 359 degrees)\n        # Saturation and Value should be 255 (100% of 255)\n        assert hue == 359, f\"Expected hue=359, got hue={hue}\"\n        assert saturation == 255, f\"Expected saturation=255, got saturation={saturation}\"\n        assert value == 255, f\"Expected value=255, got value={value}\"\n\n    def test_hsv_50_percent_hue(self):\n        \"\"\"Test that 50% hue is scaled to ~179-180, not 127.\"\"\"\n        color_parser = configtypes.QtColor()\n        parsed_color = color_parser.to_py('hsv(50%, 50%, 50%)')\n\n        hue = parsed_color.hue()\n        saturation = parsed_color.saturation()\n        value = parsed_color.value()\n\n        # 50% of 359 = 179.5, which should round to 179 or 180\n        # 50% of 255 = 127.5, which should round to 127 or 128\n        assert hue in (179, 180), f\"Expected hue in (179, 180), got hue={hue}\"\n        assert saturation in (127, 128), f\"Expected saturation in (127, 128), got saturation={saturation}\"\n        assert value in (127, 128), f\"Expected value in (127, 128), got value={value}\"\n\n    def test_hsva_100_percent_hue(self):\n        \"\"\"Test that HSVA 100% hue is scaled to 359, not 255.\"\"\"\n        color_parser = configtypes.QtColor()\n        parsed_color = color_parser.to_py('hsva(100%, 100%, 100%, 100%)')\n\n        hue = parsed_color.hue()\n        saturation = parsed_color.saturation()\n        value = parsed_color.value()\n        alpha = parsed_color.alpha()\n\n        #
